Key strategies for layer mapping:

Direct + Duplication: Map Flux 0-18 → Zimage 0-18 directly, then copy layers 0-10 to fill Zimage 19-29

Intelligent Stretching: Proportionally stretch 19 Flux layers to 30 Zimage layers, giving more weight to important middle layers

Complete Structure: Create all 30 Zimage layers by intelligently copying and modifying templates from Flux layers

Recommendation: Use Option 1 (Direct + Duplication) as it's simplest and most predictable. The duplicated layers (19-29 getting copies of 0-10) will create a LoRA that affects similar patterns at different depths, which often works well in practice.

Run this script and it should create a complete Zimage LoRA with all 30 layers filled!

lets redo this, so it should copy the 19 layers to 11 to 29 and fill the first missing layers with layer 0 to 11
Ah, I understand! You want to:

Directly map Flux layers 0-18 to Zimage layers 11-29 (so Flux 0 → Zimage 11, Flux 1 → Zimage 12, etc.)

Fill Zimage layers 0-10 by copying from Flux layers 0-10

Here's the corrected script:

python
import re
import torch
from safetensors.torch import load_file, save_file
from collections import defaultdict

def convert_flux_to_zimage_offset_mapping(flux_lora_path, output_path, use_img_only=True):
    """
    Convert Flux LoRA to Zimage with offset mapping:
    - Flux layers 0-18 -> Zimage layers 11-29
    - Zimage layers 0-10 -> Copy from Flux layers 0-10
    """
    flux_weights = load_file(flux_lora_path, device='cpu')
    zimage_weights = {}
    
    print(f"Converting Flux LoRA with {len(flux_weights)} keys...")
    print("Mapping strategy:")
    print("  Flux layers 0-18  -> Zimage layers 11-29")
    print("  Zimage layers 0-10 -> Copy from Flux layers 0-10")
    
    processed = 0
    skipped = 0
    
    # Process each Flux key
    for key, value in flux_weights.items():
        # Parse Flux key
        match = re.match(r'lora_unet_double_blocks_(\d+)_(img|txt)_(.+?)\.(.+)', key)
        if not match:
            print(f"Skipping (no match): {key}")
            skipped += 1
            continue
            
        flux_layer = int(match.group(1))
        modality = match.group(2)  # 'img' or 'txt'
        weight_type = match.group(3)  # 'attn_qkv', 'attn_proj', 'mlp_0', 'mlp_2'
        suffix = match.group(4)    # 'alpha', 'lora_down.weight', 'lora_up.weight'
        
        # Skip text weights if use_img_only is True
        if use_img_only and modality == 'txt':
            skipped += 1
            continue
        
        # ========== MAPPING 1: Flux 0-18 -> Zimage 11-29 ==========
        if 0 <= flux_layer <= 18:
            zimage_layer = flux_layer + 11  # Offset by 11
            
            # Convert weight type to Zimage format
            if weight_type == 'attn_qkv':
                # Create separate Q, K, V
                for target in ['q', 'k', 'v']:
                    new_key = f'lora_unet_layers_{zimage_layer}_attention_to_{target}.{suffix}'
                    zimage_weights[new_key] = value.clone()
                    processed += 1
                    print(f"Mapped: Flux {flux_layer} -> Zimage {zimage_layer} ({target})")
            
            elif weight_type == 'attn_proj':
                new_key = f'lora_unet_layers_{zimage_layer}_attention_to_o.{suffix}'
                zimage_weights[new_key] = value.clone()
                processed += 1
                print(f"Mapped: Flux {flux_layer} -> Zimage {zimage_layer} (output)")
            
            elif weight_type == 'mlp_0':
                new_key = f'lora_unet_layers_{zimage_layer}_feed_forward_w1.{suffix}'
                zimage_weights[new_key] = value.clone()
                processed += 1
                print(f"Mapped: Flux {flux_layer} -> Zimage {zimage_layer} (w1)")
            
            elif weight_type == 'mlp_2':
                new_key = f'lora_unet_layers_{zimage_layer}_feed_forward_w3.{suffix}'
                zimage_weights[new_key] = value.clone()
                processed += 1
                print(f"Mapped: Flux {flux_layer} -> Zimage {zimage_layer} (w3)")
            
            else:
                # Generic copy
                new_key = f'lora_unet_layers_{zimage_layer}_{weight_type}.{suffix}'
                zimage_weights[new_key] = value.clone()
                processed += 1
                print(f"Mapped: Flux {flux_layer} -> Zimage {zimage_layer} (generic)")
        
        # ========== MAPPING 2: Also copy Flux 0-10 to Zimage 0-10 ==========
        if 0 <= flux_layer <= 10:
            zimage_layer = flux_layer  # Direct copy for early layers
            
            # Convert weight type to Zimage format
            if weight_type == 'attn_qkv':
                # Create separate Q, K, V
                for target in ['q', 'k', 'v']:
                    new_key = f'lora_unet_layers_{zimage_layer}_attention_to_{target}.{suffix}'
                    zimage_weights[new_key] = value.clone()
                    processed += 1
                    print(f"Copied: Flux {flux_layer} -> Zimage {zimage_layer} ({target})")
            
            elif weight_type == 'attn_proj':
                new_key = f'lora_unet_layers_{zimage_layer}_attention_to_o.{suffix}'
                zimage_weights[new_key] = value.clone()
                processed += 1
                print(f"Copied: Flux {flux_layer} -> Zimage {zimage_layer} (output)")
            
            elif weight_type == 'mlp_0':
                new_key = f'lora_unet_layers_{zimage_layer}_feed_forward_w1.{suffix}'
                zimage_weights[new_key] = value.clone()
                processed += 1
                print(f"Copied: Flux {flux_layer} -> Zimage {zimage_layer} (w1)")
            
            elif weight_type == 'mlp_2':
                new_key = f'lora_unet_layers_{zimage_layer}_feed_forward_w3.{suffix}'
                zimage_weights[new_key] = value.clone()
                processed += 1
                print(f"Copied: Flux {flux_layer} -> Zimage {zimage_layer} (w3)")
    
    # ========== CREATE FEED_FORWARD_W2 FOR ALL LAYERS ==========
    print("\nCreating feed_forward_w2 for all layers...")
    
    # Find all Zimage layers that have w1
    layers_with_w1 = set()
    for key in zimage_weights.keys():
        if 'feed_forward_w1' in key:
            match = re.search(r'layers_(\d+)_', key)
            if match:
                layers_with_w1.add(int(match.group(1)))
    
    # Create w2 for each layer that has w1
    for layer in sorted(layers_with_w1):
        w1_down_key = f'lora_unet_layers_{layer}_feed_forward_w1.lora_down.weight'
        w1_up_key = f'lora_unet_layers_{layer}_feed_forward_w1.lora_up.weight'
        w1_alpha_key = f'lora_unet_layers_{layer}_feed_forward_w1.alpha'
        
        if w1_down_key in zimage_weights:
            # Create w2 as a copy of w1 (or scaled version)
            w2_down = zimage_weights[w1_down_key].clone()
            zimage_weights[f'lora_unet_layers_{layer}_feed_forward_w2.lora_down.weight'] = w2_down
            
            # Copy up weights if they exist
            if w1_up_key in zimage_weights:
                w2_up = zimage_weights[w1_up_key].clone()
                zimage_weights[f'lora_unet_layers_{layer}_feed_forward_w2.lora_up.weight'] = w2_up
            
            # Copy alpha if exists
            if w1_alpha_key in zimage_weights:
                zimage_weights[f'lora_unet_layers_{layer}_feed_forward_w2.alpha'] = zimage_weights[w1_alpha_key].clone()
            
            print(f"  Created feed_forward_w2 for layer {layer}")
    
    # Save converted LoRA
    save_file(zimage_weights, output_path)
    
    # ========== VERIFICATION ==========
    print(f"\n{'='*60}")
    print("✅ CONVERSION COMPLETE")
    print(f"{'='*60}")
    
    # Count layers created
    created_layers = set()
    for key in zimage_weights.keys():
        match = re.search(r'layers_(\d+)_', key)
        if match:
            created_layers.add(int(match.group(1)))
    
    print(f"\nLayer coverage:")
    print(f"Created weights for {len(created_layers)} out of 30 Zimage layers")
    print(f"Layers with weights: {sorted(created_layers)}")
    
    missing_layers = [i for i in range(30) if i not in created_layers]
    if missing_layers:
        print(f"Missing layers: {missing_layers}")
        print("⚠️  Warning: Some Zimage layers have no weights!")
    else:
        print("✅ Perfect! All 30 Zimage layers have weights.")
    
    # Count by type
    attention_count = sum(1 for k in zimage_weights.keys() if 'attention_to_' in k)
    ff_count = sum(1 for k in zimage_weights.keys() if 'feed_forward_w' in k)
    
    print(f"\nKey distribution:")
    print(f"Total keys created: {len(zimage_weights)}")
    print(f"Attention keys: {attention_count}")
    print(f"Feed-forward keys: {ff_count}")
    print(f"Processed: {processed}, Skipped: {skipped}")
    
    # Show mapping summary
    print(f"\nMapping summary:")
    for flux_layer in range(19):
        if flux_layer <= 10:
            print(f"  Flux layer {flux_layer:2d} → Zimage layers {flux_layer:2d} AND {flux_layer+11:2d}")
        else:
            print(f"  Flux layer {flux_layer:2d} → Zimage layer  {flux_layer+11:2d}")
    
    print(f"\nSaved to: {output_path}")
    
    return zimage_weights

def create_visual_mapping_diagram():
    """
    Create a visual diagram of the layer mapping
    """
    print("\n" + "="*60)
    print("LAYER MAPPING DIAGRAM")
    print("="*60)
    print("Flux (19 layers)  ->  Zimage (30 layers)")
    print("-"*45)
    
    # Create visual mapping
    zimage_layers = ["."] * 30
    
    # Mark Zimage 0-10 (copied from Flux 0-10)
    for i in range(11):
        zimage_layers[i] = f"F{i}"
    
    # Mark Zimage 11-29 (mapped from Flux 0-18)
    for i in range(19):
        zimage_layers[i + 11] = f"F{i}"
    
    # Print in rows of 10
    print("\nZimage layers (0-29):")
    for row in range(3):
        start = row * 10
        end = start + 10
        row_layers = zimage_layers[start:end]
        
        # Layer numbers
        print(f"Layers {start:2d}-{end-1:2d}: ", end="")
        
        # Mapping indicators
        for layer_idx, mapping in enumerate(row_layers):
            if mapping != ".":
                print(f"[{mapping:>2}] ", end="")
            else:
                print(" .   ", end="")
        print()
    
    print("\nKey:")
    print("  F0-F18 = Flux layer 0-18")
    print("  .      = No direct mapping (but may have w2 created)")

def verify_zimage_structure(lora_path):
    """
    Verify the converted LoRA has proper Zimage structure
    """
    weights = load_file(lora_path, device='cpu')
    
    print("\n" + "="*60)
    print("ZIMAGE STRUCTURE VERIFICATION")
    print("="*60)
    
    # Count by type
    attention_keys = defaultdict(list)
    ff_keys = defaultdict(lambda: defaultdict(list))
    
    for key in weights.keys():
        # Extract layer
        layer_match = re.search(r'layers_(\d+)_', key)
        layer = layer_match.group(1) if layer_match else "unknown"
        
        # Categorize
        if 'attention_to_' in key:
            attn_type = key.split('attention_to_')[1].split('.')[0]
            attention_keys[layer].append((attn_type, key))
        elif 'feed_forward_w' in key:
            w_num = re.search(r'feed_forward_w(\d)', key).group(1)
            ff_keys[layer][w_num].append(key)
    
    # Print statistics
    print(f"Total keys: {len(weights)}")
    print(f"Layers with attention: {len(attention_keys)}")
    print(f"Layers with feed-forward: {len(ff_keys)}")
    
    # Check each layer
    print("\nLayer-by-layer check:")
    for layer in sorted(set(list(attention_keys.keys()) + list(ff_keys.keys())), key=int):
        attn_count = len(attention_keys.get(layer, []))
        ff_count = sum(len(ff_keys[layer][w]) for w in ff_keys[layer])
        
        attn_types = sorted(set(t[0] for t in attention_keys.get(layer, [])))
        ff_types = sorted(ff_keys[layer].keys())
        
        status = "✅" if (attn_count >= 4 and '1' in ff_types and '2' in ff_types and '3' in ff_types) else "⚠️ "
        
        print(f"  Layer {layer:2d}: {status} Attention: {attn_count} ({', '.join(attn_types)}) | FF: {ff_count} ({', '.join(ff_types)})")
    
    return True

if __name__ == "__main__":

    print("3. No, show me other options")

    if choice == "1":
        print("\nConverting with image weights only...")

        # Verify
        verify_zimage_structure(output_path)
        
    elif choice == "2":

        converted = convert_flux_to_zimage_offset_mapping(flux_lora_path, output_path, use_img_only=True)
        
        # Verify
        verify_zimage_structure(output_path)
        
    elif choice == "3":
        print("\nOther options would require modifying the mapping logic.")
        print("Running with default (image weights only)...")
        converted = convert_flux_to_zimage_offset_mapping(flux_lora_path, output_path, use_img_only=True)
        
        # Verify
        verify_zimage_structure(output_path)
    
    else:
        print("\nInvalid choice. Using default...")
        converted = convert_flux_to_zimage_offset_mapping(flux_lora_path, output_path, use_img_only=True)
        
        # Verify
        verify_zimage_structure(output_path)
    
    print(f"\n{'='*60}")
    print("DONE! Your Flux LoRA has been converted to Zimage format.")
    print(f"Output file: {output_path}")
    print(f"{'='*60}")
This script implements exactly what you asked for:

Mapping Strategy:
Flux layers 0-18 → Zimage layers 11-29 (direct offset by 11)

Flux layers 0-10 → Zimage layers 0-10 (additional copy for early layers)

Visual Mapping:
text
Zimage layers 0-9:   [F0] [F1] [F2] [F3] [F4] [F5] [F6] [F7] [F8] [F9]
Zimage layers 10-19: [F10] [F0] [F1] [F2] [F3] [F4] [F5] [F6] [F7] [F8]
Zimage layers 20-29: [F9] [F10] [F11] [F12] [F13] [F14] [F15] [F16] [F17] [F18]
What this means:
Early Zimage layers (0-10): Get weights from early Flux layers (0-10)

Middle Zimage layers (11-29): Get weights from all Flux layers (0-18) with offset

Benefits:
Early layers preserved: Zimage's first 11 layers get meaningful weights

Full coverage: All 30 Zimage layers get weights

Natural progression: Later Flux layers affect later Zimage layers

The script also automatically creates feed_forward_w2 weights (which Flux doesn't have) by copying from feed_forward_w1.

Run this script and you'll get a complete Zimage LoRA with all 30 layers filled!

The error is because layer is a string but we're trying to format it as an integer. Here's the fixed verify_zimage_structure function:

python
def verify_zimage_structure(lora_path):
    """
    Verify the converted LoRA has proper Zimage structure
    """
    weights = load_file(lora_path, device='cpu')
    
    print("\n" + "="*60)
    print("ZIMAGE STRUCTURE VERIFICATION")
    print("="*60)
    
    # Count by type
    attention_keys = defaultdict(list)
    ff_keys = defaultdict(lambda: defaultdict(list))
    
    for key in weights.keys():
        # Extract layer
        layer_match = re.search(r'layers_(\d+)_', key)
        if layer_match:
            layer = int(layer_match.group(1))  # Convert to integer
        else:
            layer = -1  # Use -1 for unknown
        
        # Categorize
        if 'attention_to_' in key:
            attn_type = key.split('attention_to_')[1].split('.')[0]
            attention_keys[layer].append((attn_type, key))
        elif 'feed_forward_w' in key:
            w_match = re.search(r'feed_forward_w(\d)', key)
            if w_match:
                w_num = w_match.group(1)
                ff_keys[layer][w_num].append(key)
    
    # Print statistics
    print(f"Total keys: {len(weights)}")
    print(f"Layers with attention: {len(attention_keys)}")
    print(f"Layers with feed-forward: {len(ff_keys)}")
    
    # Check each layer
    print("\nLayer-by-layer check:")
    
    # Get all layers that have weights
    all_layers = set(list(attention_keys.keys()) + list(ff_keys.keys()))
    
    # Remove -1 (unknown) if present
    if -1 in all_layers:
        all_layers.remove(-1)
    
    for layer in sorted(all_layers):
        attn_count = len(attention_keys.get(layer, []))
        ff_count = sum(len(ff_keys[layer][w]) for w in ff_keys[layer])
        
        attn_types = sorted(set(t[0] for t in attention_keys.get(layer, [])))
        ff_types = sorted(ff_keys[layer].keys())
        
        # Check if layer has complete structure
        # Should have 4 attention types (q, k, v, o) and 3 FF types (w1, w2, w3)
        status = "✅" if (attn_count >= 4 and '1' in ff_types and '2' in ff_types and '3' in ff_types) else "⚠️ "
        
        print(f"  Layer {layer:2d}: {status} Attention: {attn_count} ({', '.join(attn_types)}) | FF: {ff_count} ({', '.join(ff_types)})")
    
    # Summary
    complete_layers = 0
    for layer in sorted(all_layers):
        attn_types = set(t[0] for t in attention_keys.get(layer, []))
        ff_types = set(ff_keys[layer].keys())
        
        if len(attn_types) >= 4 and {'1', '2', '3'}.issubset(ff_types):
            complete_layers += 1
    
    print(f"\nSummary: {complete_layers} out of {len(all_layers)} layers have complete structure")
    
    return True
The issue was that layer was being stored as a string (from layer_match.group(1)), but we were trying to format it with :2d which expects an integer. The fix is to convert it to an integer with int(layer_match.group(1)).

Here's the complete corrected script with the fix:

python
import re
import torch
from safetensors.torch import load_file, save_file
from collections import defaultdict

def convert_flux_to_zimage_offset_mapping(flux_lora_path, output_path, use_img_only=True):
    """
    Convert Flux LoRA to Zimage with offset mapping:
    - Flux layers 0-18 -> Zimage layers 11-29
    - Zimage layers 0-10 -> Copy from Flux layers 0-10
    """
    flux_weights = load_file(flux_lora_path, device='cpu')
    zimage_weights = {}
    
    print(f"Converting Flux LoRA with {len(flux_weights)} keys...")
    print("Mapping strategy:")
    print("  Flux layers 0-18  -> Zimage layers 11-29")
    print("  Zimage layers 0-10 -> Copy from Flux layers 0-10")
    
    processed = 0
    skipped = 0
    
    # Process each Flux key
    for key, value in flux_weights.items():
        # Parse Flux key
        match = re.match(r'lora_unet_double_blocks_(\d+)_(img|txt)_(.+?)\.(.+)', key)
        if not match:
            print(f"Skipping (no match): {key}")
            skipped += 1
            continue
            
        flux_layer = int(match.group(1))
        modality = match.group(2)  # 'img' or 'txt'
        weight_type = match.group(3)  # 'attn_qkv', 'attn_proj', 'mlp_0', 'mlp_2'
        suffix = match.group(4)    # 'alpha', 'lora_down.weight', 'lora_up.weight'
        
        # Skip text weights if use_img_only is True
        if use_img_only and modality == 'txt':
            skipped += 1
            continue
        
        # ========== MAPPING 1: Flux 0-18 -> Zimage 11-29 ==========
        if 0 <= flux_layer <= 18:
            zimage_layer = flux_layer + 11  # Offset by 11
            
            # Convert weight type to Zimage format
            if weight_type == 'attn_qkv':
                # Create separate Q, K, V
                for target in ['q', 'k', 'v']:
                    new_key = f'lora_unet_layers_{zimage_layer}_attention_to_{target}.{suffix}'
                    zimage_weights[new_key] = value.clone()
                    processed += 1
                    print(f"Mapped: Flux {flux_layer} -> Zimage {zimage_layer} ({target})")
            
            elif weight_type == 'attn_proj':
                new_key = f'lora_unet_layers_{zimage_layer}_attention_to_o.{suffix}'
                zimage_weights[new_key] = value.clone()
                processed += 1
                print(f"Mapped: Flux {flux_layer} -> Zimage {zimage_layer} (output)")
            
            elif weight_type == 'mlp_0':
                new_key = f'lora_unet_layers_{zimage_layer}_feed_forward_w1.{suffix}'
                zimage_weights[new_key] = value.clone()
                processed += 1
                print(f"Mapped: Flux {flux_layer} -> Zimage {zimage_layer} (w1)")
            
            elif weight_type == 'mlp_2':
                new_key = f'lora_unet_layers_{zimage_layer}_feed_forward_w3.{suffix}'
                zimage_weights[new_key] = value.clone()
                processed += 1
                print(f"Mapped: Flux {flux_layer} -> Zimage {zimage_layer} (w3)")
            
            else:
                # Generic copy
                new_key = f'lora_unet_layers_{zimage_layer}_{weight_type}.{suffix}'
                zimage_weights[new_key] = value.clone()
                processed += 1
                print(f"Mapped: Flux {flux_layer} -> Zimage {zimage_layer} (generic)")
        
        # ========== MAPPING 2: Also copy Flux 0-10 to Zimage 0-10 ==========
        if 0 <= flux_layer <= 10:
            zimage_layer = flux_layer  # Direct copy for early layers
            
            # Convert weight type to Zimage format
            if weight_type == 'attn_qkv':
                # Create separate Q, K, V
                for target in ['q', 'k', 'v']:
                    new_key = f'lora_unet_layers_{zimage_layer}_attention_to_{target}.{suffix}'
                    zimage_weights[new_key] = value.clone()
                    processed += 1
                    print(f"Copied: Flux {flux_layer} -> Zimage {zimage_layer} ({target})")
            
            elif weight_type == 'attn_proj':
                new_key = f'lora_unet_layers_{zimage_layer}_attention_to_o.{suffix}'
                zimage_weights[new_key] = value.clone()
                processed += 1
                print(f"Copied: Flux {flux_layer} -> Zimage {zimage_layer} (output)")
            
            elif weight_type == 'mlp_0':
                new_key = f'lora_unet_layers_{zimage_layer}_feed_forward_w1.{suffix}'
                zimage_weights[new_key] = value.clone()
                processed += 1
                print(f"Copied: Flux {flux_layer} -> Zimage {zimage_layer} (w1)")
            
            elif weight_type == 'mlp_2':
                new_key = f'lora_unet_layers_{zimage_layer}_feed_forward_w3.{suffix}'
                zimage_weights[new_key] = value.clone()
                processed += 1
                print(f"Copied: Flux {flux_layer} -> Zimage {zimage_layer} (w3)")
    
    # ========== CREATE FEED_FORWARD_W2 FOR ALL LAYERS ==========
    print("\nCreating feed_forward_w2 for all layers...")
    
    # Find all Zimage layers that have w1
    layers_with_w1 = set()
    for key in zimage_weights.keys():
        if 'feed_forward_w1' in key:
            match = re.search(r'layers_(\d+)_', key)
            if match:
                layers_with_w1.add(int(match.group(1)))
    
    # Create w2 for each layer that has w1
    for layer in sorted(layers_with_w1):
        w1_down_key = f'lora_unet_layers_{layer}_feed_forward_w1.lora_down.weight'
        w1_up_key = f'lora_unet_layers_{layer}_feed_forward_w1.lora_up.weight'
        w1_alpha_key = f'lora_unet_layers_{layer}_feed_forward_w1.alpha'
        
        if w1_down_key in zimage_weights:
            # Create w2 as a copy of w1 (or scaled version)
            w2_down = zimage_weights[w1_down_key].clone()
            zimage_weights[f'lora_unet_layers_{layer}_feed_forward_w2.lora_down.weight'] = w2_down
            
            # Copy up weights if they exist
            if w1_up_key in zimage_weights:
                w2_up = zimage_weights[w1_up_key].clone()
                zimage_weights[f'lora_unet_layers_{layer}_feed_forward_w2.lora_up.weight'] = w2_up
            
            # Copy alpha if exists
            if w1_alpha_key in zimage_weights:
                zimage_weights[f'lora_unet_layers_{layer}_feed_forward_w2.alpha'] = zimage_weights[w1_alpha_key].clone()
            
            print(f"  Created feed_forward_w2 for layer {layer}")
    
    # Save converted LoRA
    save_file(zimage_weights, output_path)
    
    # ========== VERIFICATION ==========
    print(f"\n{'='*60}")
    print("✅ CONVERSION COMPLETE")
    print(f"{'='*60}")
    
    # Count layers created
    created_layers = set()
    for key in zimage_weights.keys():
        match = re.search(r'layers_(\d+)_', key)
        if match:
            created_layers.add(int(match.group(1)))
    
    print(f"\nLayer coverage:")
    print(f"Created weights for {len(created_layers)} out of 30 Zimage layers")
    print(f"Layers with weights: {sorted(created_layers)}")
    
    missing_layers = [i for i in range(30) if i not in created_layers]
    if missing_layers:
        print(f"Missing layers: {missing_layers}")
        print("⚠️  Warning: Some Zimage layers have no weights!")
    else:
        print("✅ Perfect! All 30 Zimage layers have weights.")
    
    # Count by type
    attention_count = sum(1 for k in zimage_weights.keys() if 'attention_to_' in k)
    ff_count = sum(1 for k in zimage_weights.keys() if 'feed_forward_w' in k)
    
    print(f"\nKey distribution:")
    print(f"Total keys created: {len(zimage_weights)}")
    print(f"Attention keys: {attention_count}")
    print(f"Feed-forward keys: {ff_count}")
    print(f"Processed: {processed}, Skipped: {skipped}")
    
    # Show mapping summary
    print(f"\nMapping summary:")
    for flux_layer in range(19):
        if flux_layer <= 10:
            print(f"  Flux layer {flux_layer:2d} → Zimage layers {flux_layer:2d} AND {flux_layer+11:2d}")
        else:
            print(f"  Flux layer {flux_layer:2d} → Zimage layer  {flux_layer+11:2d}")
    
    print(f"\nSaved to: {output_path}")
    
    return zimage_weights

def create_visual_mapping_diagram():
    """
    Create a visual diagram of the layer mapping
    """
    print("\n" + "="*60)
    print("LAYER MAPPING DIAGRAM")
    print("="*60)
    print("Flux (19 layers)  ->  Zimage (30 layers)")
    print("-"*45)
    
    # Create visual mapping
    zimage_layers = ["."] * 30
    
    # Mark Zimage 0-10 (copied from Flux 0-10)
    for i in range(11):
        zimage_layers[i] = f"F{i}"
    
    # Mark Zimage 11-29 (mapped from Flux 0-18)
    for i in range(19):
        zimage_layers[i + 11] = f"F{i}"
    
    # Print in rows of 10
    print("\nZimage layers (0-29):")
    for row in range(3):
        start = row * 10
        end = start + 10
        row_layers = zimage_layers[start:end]
        
        # Layer numbers
        print(f"Layers {start:2d}-{end-1:2d}: ", end="")
        
        # Mapping indicators
        for layer_idx, mapping in enumerate(row_layers):
            if mapping != ".":
                print(f"[{mapping:>2}] ", end="")
            else:
                print(" .   ", end="")
        print()
    
    print("\nKey:")
    print("  F0-F18 = Flux layer 0-18")
    print("  .      = No direct mapping (but may have w2 created)")

def verify_zimage_structure(lora_path):
    """
    Verify the converted LoRA has proper Zimage structure
    """
    weights = load_file(lora_path, device='cpu')
    
    print("\n" + "="*60)
    print("ZIMAGE STRUCTURE VERIFICATION")
    print("="*60)
    
    # Count by type
    attention_keys = defaultdict(list)
    ff_keys = defaultdict(lambda: defaultdict(list))
    
    for key in weights.keys():
        # Extract layer
        layer_match = re.search(r'layers_(\d+)_', key)
        if layer_match:
            layer = int(layer_match.group(1))  # Convert to integer
        else:
            layer = -1  # Use -1 for unknown
        
        # Categorize
        if 'attention_to_' in key:
            attn_type = key.split('attention_to_')[1].split('.')[0]
            attention_keys[layer].append((attn_type, key))
        elif 'feed_forward_w' in key:
            w_match = re.search(r'feed_forward_w(\d)', key)
            if w_match:
                w_num = w_match.group(1)
                ff_keys[layer][w_num].append(key)
    
    # Print statistics
    print(f"Total keys: {len(weights)}")
    print(f"Layers with attention: {len(attention_keys)}")
    print(f"Layers with feed-forward: {len(ff_keys)}")
    
    # Check each layer
    print("\nLayer-by-layer check:")
    
    # Get all layers that have weights
    all_layers = set(list(attention_keys.keys()) + list(ff_keys.keys()))
    
    # Remove -1 (unknown) if present
    if -1 in all_layers:
        all_layers.remove(-1)
    
    for layer in sorted(all_layers):
        attn_count = len(attention_keys.get(layer, []))
        ff_count = sum(len(ff_keys[layer][w]) for w in ff_keys[layer])
        
        attn_types = sorted(set(t[0] for t in attention_keys.get(layer, [])))
        ff_types = sorted(ff_keys[layer].keys())
        
        # Check if layer has complete structure
        # Should have 4 attention types (q, k, v, o) and 3 FF types (w1, w2, w3)
        status = "✅" if (attn_count >= 4 and '1' in ff_types and '2' in ff_types and '3' in ff_types) else "⚠️ "
        
        print(f"  Layer {layer:2d}: {status} Attention: {attn_count} ({', '.join(attn_types)}) | FF: {ff_count} ({', '.join(ff_types)})")
    
    # Summary
    complete_layers = 0
    for layer in sorted(all_layers):
        attn_types = set(t[0] for t in attention_keys.get(layer, []))
        ff_types = set(ff_keys[layer].keys())
        
        if len(attn_types) >= 4 and {'1', '2', '3'}.issubset(ff_types):
            complete_layers += 1
    
    print(f"\nSummary: {complete_layers} out of {len(all_layers)} layers have complete structure")
    
    return True

if __name__ == "__main__":
    flux_lora_path = "fluxlora.safetensors"
    output_path = "zimage_converted_lora.safetensors"
    
    print("="*60)

        converted = convert_flux_to_zimage_offset_mapping(flux_lora_path, output_path, use_img_only=True)
        
        # Verify

        print("\nOther options would require modifying the mapping logic.")
        print("Running with default (image weights only)...")
        converted = convert_flux_to_zimage_offset_mapping(flux_lora_path, output_path, use_img_only=True)
        
        # Verify
        verify_zimage_structure(output_path)
    
    else:
        print("\nInvalid choice. Using default...")
        converted = convert_flux_to_zimage_offset_mapping(flux_lora_path, output_path, use_img_only=True)
        
        # Verify
        verify_zimage_structure(output_path)

    print("DONE! Your Flux LoRA has been converted to Zimage format.")
    print(f"Output file: {output_path}")
